          skip_if: raw.skip_if,\n   294\t        })\n   295\t    }\n   296\t}\n   297\t\n   298\t/// Parse and validate injection mode from raw fields.\n   299\tfn parse_inject_mode(\n   300\t    after: &Option<String>,\n   301\t    before: &Option<String>,\n   302\t    prepend: bool,\n   303\t    append: bool,\n   304\t    at: &Option<String>,\n   305\t    index: usize,\n   306\t    source: &Path,\n   307\t) -> Result<InjectMode, JigError> {\n   308\t    let loc = format!(\"files[{index}] in {}\", source.display());\n   309\t\n   310\t    let mode_count = [after.is_some(), before.is_some(), prepend, append]\n   311\t        .iter()\n   312\t        .filter(|&&b| b)\n   313\t        .count();\n   314\t\n   315\t    if mode_count == 0 {\n   316\t        return Err(recipe_err(\n   317\t            \"inject operation missing mode\",\n   318\t            &loc,\n   319\t            \"inject must specify one of: 'after', 'before', 'prepend: true', or 'append: true'\",\n   320\t            \"add an injection mode field\",\n   321\t        ));\n   322\t    }\n   323\t    if mode_count > 1 {\n   324\t        return Err(recipe_err(\n   325\t            \"inject operation has conflicting modes\",\n   326\t            &loc,\n   327\t            \"only one of 'after', 'before', 'prepend', 'append' may be specified\",\n   328\t            \"remove extra injection mode fields so only one remains\",\n   329\t        ));\n   330\t    }\n   331\t\n   332\t    if let Some(pattern) = after {\n   333\t        let pos = parse_match_position(at, index, source)?;\n   334\t        validate_regex(pattern, \"after\", index, source)?;\n   335\t        Ok(InjectMode::After { pattern: pattern.clone(), at: pos })\n   336\t    } else if let Some(pattern) = before {\n   337\t        let pos = parse_match_position(at, index, source)?;\n   338\t        validate_regex(pattern, \"before\", index, source)?;\n   339\t        Ok(InjectMode::Before { pattern: pattern.clone(), at: pos })\n   340\t    } else if prepend {\n   341\t        Ok(InjectMode::Prepend)\n   342\t    } else {\n   343\t        Ok(InjectMode::Append)\n   344\t    }\n   345\t}\n   346\t\n   347\tfn parse_match_position(\n   348\t    at: &Option<String>,\n   349\t    _index: usize,\n   350\t    _source: &Path,\n   351\t) -> Result<MatchPosition, JigError> {\n   352\t    match at.as_deref() {\n   353\t        None | Some(\"first\") => Ok(MatchPosition::First),\n   354\t        Some(\"last\") => Ok(MatchPosition::Last),\n   355\t        Some(other) => Err(recipe_err(\n   356\t            &format!(\"invalid 'at' value: '{other}'\"),\n   357\t            &format!(\"files[{_index}] in {}\", _source.display()),\n   358\t            \"at must be 'first' or 'last'\",\n   359\t            \"use at: first or at: last\",\n   360\t        )),\n   361\t    }\n   362\t}\n   363\t\n   364\tfn validate_regex(pattern: &str, field: &str, index: usize, source: &Path) -> Result<(), JigError> {\n   365\t    regex::Regex::new(pattern).map_err(|e| recipe_err(\n   366\t        &format!(\"invalid regex in '{field}' field\"),\n   367\t        &format!(\"files[{index}] in {}\", source.display()),\n   368\t        &format!(\"pattern '{pattern}' failed to compile: {e}\"),\n   369\t        \"check regex syntax — remember to escape special characters\",\n   370\t    ))?;\n   371\t    Ok(())\n   372\t}\n   373\t\n   374\tfn recipe_err(what: &str, where_: &str, why: &str, hint: &str) -> JigError {\n   375\t    JigError::RecipeValidation(StructuredError {\n   376\t        what: what.to_string(),\n   377\t        where_: where_.to_string(),\n   378\t        why: why.to_string(),\n   379\t        hint: hint.to_string(),\n   380\t    })\n   381\t}\n   382\t\n   383\t// ── Tests ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n   384\t\n   385\t#[cfg(test)]\n   386\tmod tests {\n   387\t    use super::*;\n   388\t    use std::fs;\n   389\t    use tempfile::TempDir;\n   390\t\n   391\t    /// Helper: create a temp recipe directory with given files.\n   392\t    fn setup_recipe(yaml: &str, templates: &[&str]) -> (TempDir, PathBuf) {\n   393\t        let dir = TempDir::new().unwrap();\n   394\t        let recipe_path = dir.path().join(\"recipe.yaml\");\n   395\t        fs::write(&recipe_path, yaml).unwrap();\n   396\t        for t in templates {\n   397\t            let p = dir.path().join(t);\n   398\t            if let Some(parent) = p.parent() {\n   399\t                fs::create_dir_all(parent).unwrap();\n   400\t            }\n   401\t            fs::write(&p, \"template content\").unwrap();\n   402\t        }\n   403\t        (dir, recipe_path)\n   404\t    }\n   405\t\n   406\t    // ── FR-1 acceptance criteria undefined variable in a template by scanning for references\n   147\t/// not present in the variable context.\n   148\tfn find_undefined_variable(template_source: &str, error_line: Option<usize>, vars: &Value) -> String {\n   149\t    let var_keys: Vec<&str> = match vars.as_object() {\n   150\t        Some(obj) => obj.keys().map(|s| s.as_str()).collect(),\n   151\t        None => vec![],\n   152\t    };\n   153\t\n   154\t    // Extract variable references from the template.\n   155\t    // Matches {{ name }}, {{ name | filter }}, {{ name.attr }}, etc.\n   156\t    let re = regex::Regex::new(r\"\\{\\{[\\s-]*([a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9_]*)\").unwrap();\n   157\t    // Also check {% if/for/elif blocks\n   158\t    let block_re =  164\t        let line = lines[line_num - 1];\n   165\t        for cap in re.captures_iter(line).chain(block_re.captures_iter(line)) {\n   166\t            let name = &cap[1];\n   167\t            if !var_keys.contains(&name) {\n   168\t                return name.to_string();\n   169\t            }\n   170\t        }\n   171\t    }\n   172\t\n   173\t    // Fall back to scanning the entire template\n   174\t    for cap in re.captures_iter(template_source).chain(block_re.captures_iter(template_source)) {\n   175\t        let name = &cap[1];\n   176\t        if !var_keys.contains(&name) {\n   177\t            return name.to_string();\n   178\t        }\n   179\t    }\n   180\t\n   181\t    \"unknown\".to_string()\n   182\t}\n   183\t\n   184\t/// Generate a \"did you mean?\" hint using Levenshtein distance.\n   185\t/// Looks at all keys in the provided variable context.\n   186\tfn did_you_mean_hint(var_name: &str, vars: &Value) -> String {\n   187\t    let keys: Vec<&str> = 191\t\n   192\t    if keys.is_empty() {\n   193\t        return format!(\"check variable name '{}' — no variables were provided\", var_name);\n   194\t    }\n   195\t\n   196\t    let mut best_match:   89\t/// A path appears in files_skipped only if ALL operations targeting it were skipped.\n    90\t/// Paths appear in order of first encounter.\n    91\tfn compute_file_summaries(results: 210\t#[allow(clippy::too_many_arguments)]\n   211\tfn cmd_run(\n   212\t    recipe_path: &std::path::Path,\n   213\t    inline_vars: Option<&str>,\n   214\t    vars_file: Option<&std::path::Path>,\n verbose: bool,\n   222\t) -> Result<i32, JigError> {\n   223\t    // 1. Load and validate recipe (exit 1 on failure).\n   224\t    let recipe = Recipe::load(recipe_path)?;\n   225\t\n   226\t    // 2. Collect and validate variables (exit 4 on failure).\n   227\t    let provided = variables::collect_vars(inline_vars, vars_file, vars_stdin)?;\n   228\t    let vars = variables::validate_variables(&recipe.variables, &provided)?;\n   229\t\n   230\t    // 3. Validate base_dir exists (AC-4.10).\n   231\t    let resolved_base = match base_dir {\n   232\t        Some(bd) => {\n   233\t            if !bd.is_dir() {\n   234\t                return Err(JigError::FileOperation(crate::error::StructuredError {\n   235\t                    what: format!(\"base directory does not exist: '{}'\", bd.display()),\n   236\t                    where_: bd.display().to_string(),\n   237\t                    why: \"the specified --base-dir path is not an existing directory\".into(),\n   238\t                    hint: \"create the directory first, or omit --base-dir to use the current directory\".into(),\n   239\t                }));\n   240\t            }\n   241\t            bd.to_path_buf()\n   242\t        }\n   243\t        None => std::env::current_dir().unwrap_or_else(|_| PathBuf::from(\".\")),\n   244\t    };\n   245\t\n   246\t    // 4. Create recipe-aware environment and render ALL templates upfront (exit 2 on failure).\n   247\t    let env = renderer::create_recipe_env(&recipe)?;\n   248\t\n   249\t    let mut prepared_ops = Vec::with_capacity(recipe.files.len());\n   250\t    for (i, file_op) in recipe.files.iter().enumerate() {\n   251\t        // Render the template content.\n   252\t        let rendered_content = renderer::render_template(&env, file_op.template(), &vars)?;\n   253\t\n   254\t        // Render templated path fields.\n   255\t        let rendered_path = match file_op {\n   256\t            recipe::FileOp::Create { to, .. } => {\n   257\t                renderer::render_path_template(&env, to, &vars, &format!(\"files[{}].to\", i))?\n   258\t            }\n   259\t            recipe::FileOp::Inject { inject, .. } => {\n   260\t                renderer::render_path_template(&env, inject, &vars, &format!(\"files[{}].inject\", i))?\n   261\t            }\n   262\t        };\n   263\t\n   264\t        // Render skip_if for inject operations.\n   265\t        let rendered_skip_if = match file_op {\n   266\t            recipe::FileOp::Inject { skip_if: Some(skip_if_expr), .. } => {\n   267\t                Some(renderer::render_path_template(\n   268\t                    &env, skip_if_expr, &vars, &format!(\"files[{}].skip_if\", i),\n   269\t                )?)\n   270\t            }\n   271\t            _ => None,\n   272\t        };\n   273\t\n   274\t        prepared_ops.push(operations::PreparedOp {\n   275\t            file_op: file_op.clone(),\n   276\t            rendered_content,\n   277\t            rendered_path,\n   278\t            rendered_skip_if,\n   279\t        });\n   280\t    }\n   281\t\n   282\t    // 5. Execute operations in declaration order, fail-fast on error.\n   283\t    let mut ctx = operations::ExecutionContext::new(resolved_base, dry_run, force);\n   284\t    let mut results: Vec<operations::OpResult> = Vec::with_capacity(prepared_ops.len());\n   285\t\n   286\t    for prepared in &prepared_ops {\n   287\t        let result = operations::execute_operation(prepared, &mut ctx, verbose);\n   288\t        let is_err = result.is_error();\n   289\t        results.push(result);\n   290\t        if is_err {\n   291\t            break; // Fail-fast: stop on first error (AC-6.10).\n   292\t        }\n   293\t    }\n   294\t\n   295\t    // 6. Format and emit output.\n   296\t    let mode = output::detect_mode(force_json);\n   297\t    let has_error = results.iter().any(|r| r.is_error());\n   298\t\n   299\t    match mode {\n   300\t        output::OutputMode::Json => {\n   301\t            let json = output::format_json(&results, dry_run, verbose);\n   302\t            println!(\"{}\", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&json).unwrap());\n   303\t        }\n   304\t        output::OutputMode::Human => {\n   305\t            if !quiet {\n   306\t                output::format_human(&results, dry_run, verbose);\n   307\t            }\n   308\t        }\n   309\t    }\n   310\t\n   311\t    // 7. Return appropriate exit code.\n   312\t    // Error details are already in the JSON/human output above, so return Ok\n   313\t    // with the exit code to avoid duplicate stderr output from main().\n   314\t    if has_error {\n   315\t        if let Some(last) = results.last()\n   316\t            && let Some(jig_err) = operations::op_error_to_jig_error(last) {\n   317\t                return Ok(jig_err.exit_code());\n   318\t            }\n   319\t    }\n   320\t\n   321\t    Ok(0)\n   322\t}\n   323\t\n   324\tfn build_validate_json(recipe: &Recipe) -> serde_json::Value {\n   325\t {"type":"item.completed","item":{"id":"item_42","type":"agent_message","text":"**Verdict:** Request Changes\n\n**Critical**\n- `--quiet` is not honored for `jig run` errors that occur before operation execution. `run` returns `Err` for recipe/vars/template/base-dir failures, and `main()` unconditionally writes to stderr (`eprintln!`) on any `Err`, so stderr is still emitted with `--quiet`. This violates AC-6.4 / AC-6.9 and invariant I-8.  \n  [src/main.rs#L95](/Users/tylerobriant/code/tetra/jig/src/main.rs#L95), [src/main.rs#L224](/Users/tylerobriant/code/tetra/jig/src/main.rs#L224), [src/main.rs#L305](/Users/tylerobriant/code/tetra/jig/src/main.rs#L305)\n\n- Exit-code stage ordering is wrong when `--base-dir` is invalid and templates are also invalid. Base-dir validation (file-op category, code 3) runs before template rendering (code 2), so code 3 wins incorrectly. This violates AC-N5.2 / I-5 (stable exit-code contract by first failing stage).  \n  [src/main.rs#L230](/Users/tylerobriant/code/tetra/jig/src/main.rs#L230), [src/main.rs#L246](/Users/tylerobriant/code/tetra/jig/src/main.rs#L246)\n\n- Inject accepts empty regex patterns (`after: \"\"` / `before: \"\"`) as valid. `parse_inject_mode` forwards empty strings to `validate_regex`, and `Regex::new(\"\")` succeeds, causing silent “match everywhere” behavior instead of validation failure. This violates AC-5.13 and conflicts with I-10 (fail clearly, don’t silently do the wrong thing).  \n  [src/recipe.rs#L332](/Users/tylerobriant/code/tetra/jig/src/recipe.rs#L332), [src/recipe.rs#L364](/Users/tylerobriant/code/tetra/jig/src/recipe.rs#L364)\n\n**Major**\n- None.\n\n**Minor**\n- Human error output only shows `rendered_content` when non-empty; with empty rendered content it omits the section, which is weaker than AC-N4.2’s “always include rendered content on file-op errors.”  \n  [src/output.rs#L166](/Users/tylerobriant/code/tetra/jig/src/output.rs#L166)\n\n**Strengths**\n- Render-all-upfront before execution is implemented cleanly and matches the spec intent to avoid partial writes from template/render failures.\n- Dry-run virtual file state correctly supports create→inject chaining and cumulative inject behavior.\n- JSON `files_written` / `files_skipped` summary logic preserves first-seen order and avoids duplicate paths."}}
